namespace = tec_ascension

 # Generic
	situation_event = { # this is done to avoid apparently 200=0 not working for situations
		id = tec_ascension.404
		hide_window = yes
		is_triggered_only = yes
		#situation = this

		trigger = {
			always = no
		}
	}
	country_event = {	# TODO ASCENSION TEST CUI
		id = tec_ascension.606
		title = "tec_ascension.100.name"
		desc = "tec_ascension.100.desc.regular"
		diplomatic = yes
		custom_gui = tec_gui_ascension_event
		is_triggered_only = yes
		immediate = {
			set_global_flag = tec_test_gui_genetics
			set_global_flag = tec_test_gui
			remove_global_flag = tec_test_gui
		}
		option = {
			name = OK
		}
	}

 # On ap pick - on_ascension_perk_picked
	# tec_ascension.10 > 100 = biological
	# tec_ascension.20 > 200 = cybernetic
	# tec_ascension.30 > 300 = synthetic
	# tec_ascension.40 > 400 = mystical
	country_event = { # Engineered Evolution picked
		id = tec_ascension.10
		hide_window = yes

		is_triggered_only = yes

		trigger = {
			has_ascension_perk = ap_engineered_evolution
			NOR = {
				has_country_flag = ap_engineered_evolution
				has_country_flag = ap_engineered_evolution_genetics
				has_country_flag = ap_engineered_evolution_biogenics
			}
		}

		immediate = {
			set_country_flag = ap_engineered_evolution
			# Global controller
				event_target:global_event_country = {
					change_variable = {
						which = tec_number_of_bioascended_empires
						value = 1
					}
				}
			# /
			# Situation
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = tec_advanced_ascension
					}
					tec_give_t1_genetics_effect = yes
				}
				else = {
					country_event = {
						id = tec_ascension.100
					}
				}
			# /
			# Techs
				if = {	# Gene Tailoring
					limit = {
						NOR = {
							has_tech_option = tech_gene_tailoring
							has_technology = tech_gene_tailoring
						}
					}
					add_research_option = tech_gene_tailoring
				}
				if = { # Gene Seed
					limit = {
						NOR = {
							has_tech_option = tech_gene_seed_purification
							has_technology = tech_gene_seed_purification
						}
					}
					add_research_option = tech_gene_seed_purification
				}
			# /
			# Fear of the Dark Separatists - Scared
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_origin = origin_fear_of_the_dark
						any_planet_within_border = {
							has_planet_flag = fotd_seperatist_planet@root
							owner = {
								has_country_flag = fotd_seperatist_country@root
							}
						}
					}
					country_event = { id = origin.6115 days = 10 random = 5 }
				}
			# /
		}
	}
	country_event = { # The FLesh Is Weak picked
		id = tec_ascension.20
		hide_window = yes

		is_triggered_only = yes

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_ascension_perk = ap_the_flesh_is_weak
				has_ascension_perk = ap_organo_machine_interfacing
				has_ascension_perk = ap_organo_machine_interfacing_assimilator
			}
			NOR = {
				has_country_flag = ap_the_flesh_is_weak
				has_country_flag = ap_the_flesh_is_weak_cybernetics
				has_country_flag = ap_the_flesh_is_weak_bioware
			}
		}

		immediate = {
			set_country_flag = ap_the_flesh_is_weak
			# Global controller
				event_target:global_event_country = {
					change_variable = {
						which = tec_number_of_technoascended_empires
						value = 1
					}
				}
			# /
			# Situation
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = tec_advanced_ascension
					}
					tec_give_t1_cybernetics_effect = yes
				}
				else = {
					country_event = {
						id = tec_ascension.200
					}
				}
			# /
			# Techs
				if = {	# Neuro Quantum Links
					limit = {
						NOR = {
							has_tech_option = tech_neuro_quantum_links
							has_technology = tech_neuro_quantum_links
						}
					}
					add_research_option = tech_neuro_quantum_links
				}
			# /
			# Fear of the Dark Separatists - Scared
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_planet_within_border = {
							has_planet_flag = fotd_seperatist_planet@root
							owner = {
								has_country_flag = fotd_seperatist_country@root
							}
						}
					}
					country_event = { id = origin.6095 days = 10 random = 10 }
				}
			# /
		}
	}
	country_event = { # Synthetic Evolution picked
		id = tec_ascension.30
		hide_window = yes

		is_triggered_only = yes

		trigger = {

			NOR = {

		immediate = {

			# Global controller
				event_target:global_event_country = {
					change_variable = {
						which = tec_number_of_technoascended_empires

			# Situation

					limit = {

					}
					tec_give_t1_synthetics_effect = yes
				}
				else = {
					country_event = {
						id = tec_ascension.300
					}
				}
			# /	
			# Techs
				if = {	# Synthetic Workers
					limit = {
						NOR = {
							has_tech_option = tech_synthetic_workers
							has_technology = tech_synthetic_workers
						}
					}

				}
				if = {	# Synthetic leaders
					limit = {
						NOR = {
							has_tech_option = tech_synthetic_leaders
							has_technology = tech_synthetic_leaders
						}
					}
					add_research_option = tech_synthetic_leaders
				}
			# /

	}
	country_event = { # Mind Over Matter picked
		id = tec_ascension.40
		hide_window = yes

		is_triggered_only = yes

		trigger = {
			has_ascension_perk = ap_mind_over_matter
			NOR = {
				has_country_flag = ap_mind_over_matter
				has_country_flag = ap_mind_over_matter_psionic
				has_country_flag = ap_mind_over_matter_psychic
				has_country_flag = ap_mind_over_matter_psionic_ethereal
				has_country_flag = ap_mind_over_matter_psychic_ethereal
			}
		}

		immediate = {
			set_country_flag = ap_mind_over_matter
			# Global controller
				event_target:global_event_country = {
					change_variable = {
						which = tec_number_of_mystical_empires
						value = 1
					}
				}
			# /
			# Situation
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_hive_empire = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = tec_advanced_ascension
						}
						tec_give_t1_psychic_effect = yes
					}
					else = {
						country_event = {
							id = tec_ascension.410
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = tec_advanced_ascension
						}
						tec_give_t1_psionic_effect = yes
					}
					else = {
						country_event = {
							id = tec_ascension.400
						}
					}
				}
			# /
			# Techs
				if = {	# Psi Theory
					limit = {
						NOR = {
							has_tech_option = tech_psionic_theory
							has_technology = tech_psionic_theory
						}
					}
					add_research_option = tech_psionic_theory
				}
				if = { # Telepathy
					limit = {
						is_gestalt = no
						NOR = {
							has_tech_option = tech_telepathy
							has_technology = tech_telepathy
						}
					}
					custom_tooltip = tec_ap_unlock_tech_telepathy
					hidden_effect = {
						add_research_option = tech_telepathy
					}
				}
			# /
		}
	}
	country_event = { # Synthetic Age picked

 # Gate situations
  # Biological paths gate - 100
	country_event = { # Engineered Evolution picked
		id = tec_ascension.100
		title = "tec_ascension.100.name"
		# Descs
			# Regular
			desc = {
				text = "tec_ascension.100.desc.regular"
				trigger = {
					is_gestalt = no
					NOR = {
						has_origin = origin_clone_army
						has_origin = origin_necrophage
						AND = {
							has_origin = origin_syncretic_evolution
							has_valid_civic = civic_tec_origin_elders
						}
					}
				}
			}
			desc = {
				text = "tec_ascension.100.desc.origin_clone_army"
				trigger = {
					is_gestalt = no
					has_origin = origin_clone_army
				}
			}
			desc = {
				text = "tec_ascension.100.desc.origin_necrophage"
				trigger = {
					is_gestalt = no
					has_origin = origin_necrophage
				}
			}
			desc = {
				text = "tec_ascension.100.desc.civic_tec_origin_elders"
				trigger = {
					is_gestalt = no
					AND = {
						has_origin = origin_syncretic_evolution
						has_valid_civic = civic_tec_origin_elders
					}
				}
			}
			# Hive
			desc = {
				text = "tec_ascension.100.desc.hive"
				trigger = {
					is_hive_empire = yes
				}
			}
		# /
		picture = GFX_evt_genetic_modification
		show_sound = event_engineered_evolution
		trackable = yes

		is_triggered_only = yes

		immediate = {
			hidden_effect = {
				save_event_target_as = tec_target_country
				event_target:tec_target_country = {
					start_situation = {
						type = situation_tec_ascension_biological_neutral_t1
						target = event_target:tec_target_country.capital_scope
						effect = {
							save_event_target_as = new_situation
						}
					}
					event_target:new_situation = {
						set_situation_locked = yes
						set_situation_approach = situation_tec_ascension_biological_neutral_t1_approach_standard
					}
				}
			}
		}

		after = {
			hidden_effect = {
				event_target:new_situation = {
					set_situation_locked = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					hidden_trigger = {
						always = no
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = "tec_situation_slower_notech_biological"
			}
		}

		# Options
			# Regular
			option = {	# Slow
				name = "tec_ascension.100.approach.slow.regular"
				custom_tooltip = "tec_ascension.100.approach.slow.regular.tooltip"
				icon = {
					icon = GFX_situation_approach_genetics
					icon_background = GFX_situation_approach_bg_green
					text = tec_icon_text_approach_slow
				}
				trigger = {
					hidden_trigger = {
						is_gestalt = no
					}
				}
				event_target:new_situation = {
					set_situation_locked = yes
					set_situation_approach = situation_tec_ascension_biological_neutral_t1_approach_slow
				}
			}
			option = {	# Standard
				name = "tec_ascension.100.approach.standard.regular"
				custom_tooltip = "tec_ascension.100.approach.standard.regular.tooltip"
				icon = {
					icon = GFX_situation_approach_research

	# Situation
	situation_event = { # 10% - first indication
		id = tec_ascension.10010
		title = "tec_ascension.10010.name"
		# Desc
			# Regular
			desc = {	# Regular
				text = "tec_ascension.10010.desc.regular"
				trigger = {
					exists = owner

						is_gestalt = no
						NOR = {
							has_origin = origin_clone_army
							has_origin = origin_necrophage
							AND = {
								has_origin = origin_syncretic_evolution
								has_valid_civic = civic_tec_origin_elders
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}

					exists = owner
					owner = {
						is_gestalt = no

					}
				}
			}
			desc = {	# Necro
				text = "tec_ascension.10010.desc.origin_necrophage"

				}

				trigger = {

		immediate = {
			hidden_effect = {
				save_event_target_as = tec_target_country
				event_target:tec_target_country = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_hive_empire = yes
						}
						start_situation = {
							type = situation_tec_ascension_mystical_neutral_t1_hive
							target = event_target:tec_target_country.capital_scope
							effect = {
								save_event_target_as = new_situation
							}
						}
						event_target:new_situation = {
							set_situation_locked = yes
							set_situation_approach = situation_tec_ascension_mystical_neutral_t1_hive_approach_standard
						}
					}
					else = {
						start_situation = {
							type = situation_tec_ascension_mystical_neutral_t1
							target = event_target:tec_target_country.capital_scope
							effect = {

		id = tec_cybernetic_path.110
		hide_window = yes

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_tradition = tr_cybernetics_adopt
				has_tradition = tr_cybernetics_assimilator_adopt
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = tec_adopted_tradition_cybernetics
			}
		}
		immediate = {
			# Safeproofing flag
			set_country_flag = tec_adopted_tradition_cybernetics
			if = {		# MAge - Cyberization situation (regular)
				limit = {
					has_machine_age_dlc = yes
					NOT = {
						has_origin = origin_cybernetic_creed
					}
				}
				if = { # Assimilators
					limit = {
						has_machine_age_dlc = yes
						has_civic = civic_machine_assimilator
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						country_event = {
							id = cyber.2010
							days = 2
						}
					}
				}
				else = { # Non assimilators and etc
					country_event = {
						id = cyber.1
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {	# MAge - Cybernetic creed
				limit = {
					has_machine_age_dlc = yes
					has_origin = origin_cybernetic_creed
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = {
						id = machine_age.100
					}
				}
			}
			else = {	# No MAge - Gives cybernetics
				hidden_effect = {
					# OG is utopia.2500
					country_event = {
						id = tec_cybernetic_path.11010
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

  # --------------- SYNTH T1 situation
	situation_event = { # Synth T1 - 50
		id = tec_synth_path.10050
		title = "tec_synth_path.10050.name"
		# Descs
			# Regular
			desc = {	# Regular
				text = "tec_synth_path.10050.desc.regular"
				trigger = {
					owner = {
						is_gestalt = no
						NOT = {
							has_origin = origin_synthetic_fertility
						}
					}
				}
			}
			# Synth Fertility
			desc = {	# Regular
				text = "tec_synth_path.10050.desc.synthetic.fertility"
				trigger = {
					owner = {
						is_gestalt = no
						NOT = {
							has_origin = origin_synthetic_fertility
						}
					}
				}
			}
			# No robots?
			desc = {	# Regular
				text = "tec_synth_path.10050.desc.no.robots"
				trigger = {
					always = no
				}
			}
		# /
		picture = GFX_evt_cybernetics
		is_triggered_only = yes
		situation = this
		location = target

		immediate = {
			hidden_effect = {
				set_situation_locked = yes
			}
		}

		after = {
			hidden_effect = {
				set_situation_locked = no
				owner = {
					# Marks the robotic species
					random_owned_species = {
						limit = {
							has_trait = trait_mechanical
							OR = {
								has_species_flag = mechanical_species@prev
								has_species_flag = mechanical_species_fake_@prev
							}
						}
						save_event_target_as = tec_robot_unit
					}
				}
			}
		}

		# Options
			# Regular
			option = {	# Regular
				name = "tec_synth_path.10050.new.bodies"
				custom_tooltip = "tec_synth_path.10050.new.bodies.tooltip"
				icon = {
					icon = GFX_situation_approach_tec_gear
					icon_background = GFX_situation_approach_bg_tec_blue
					text = tec_situation_important_decision
				}
				trigger = {
					hidden_trigger = {
						exists = owner
						owner = {
							NOT = {
								has_origin = origin_synthetic_fertility
							}
						}
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_situation_flag = tec_synth_new_bodies
					owner = {
						set_country_flag = tec_synth_new_bodies
					}
				}
			}
			option = {	# Regular
				name = "tec_synth_path.10050.use.robots"
				custom_tooltip = "tec_synth_path.10050.use.robots.tooltip"
				icon = {
					icon = GFX_situation_approach_tec_ai
					icon_background = GFX_situation_approach_bg_tec_blue
					text = tec_situation_important_decision
				}
				trigger = {
					hidden_trigger = {
						exists = owner
						owner = {
							any_owned_species = {
								has_trait = trait_mechanical
								OR = {
									has_species_flag = mechanical_species@prev
									has_species_flag = mechanical_species_fake_@prev
								}
							}
							NOT = {
								has_origin = origin_synthetic_fertility
							}
						}
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_situation_flag = tec_synth_use_robots
					owner = {
						set_country_flag = tec_synth_use_robots
					}
				}
			}
			# Synthetic Fertility
			option = {	# Regular
				name = "tec_synth_path.10050.ok.synthetic.fertility"
				custom_tooltip = "tec_synth_path.10050.ok.synthetic.fertility.tooltip"
				icon = {
					icon = GFX_situation_approach_tec_ai
					icon_background = GFX_situation_approach_bg_tec_blue
					text = tec_situation_continues_good
				}
				trigger = {
					hidden_trigger = {
						exists = owner

	situation_event = { # Synth T1 - 70 - Sorter
		id = tec_synth_path.10070
		title = "tec_synth_path.10070.name"
		# Descs
			# Regular
			desc = {	# Regular
				text = "tec_synth_path.10070.desc.regular"
			}
		# /
		picture = GFX_evt_cybernetics
		is_triggered_only = yes
		situation = this
		location = target

		immediate = {
			hidden_effect = {
				set_situation_locked = yes
			}
		}

		after = {
			hidden_effect = {
				set_situation_locked = no
				# Sort outcomes
					#tec_variable_score_sorter = {
					#	VARIABLE = tec_synth_path_score
					#	CLEAR_VAR = yes
					#	ELEMENT_1 = "has_situation_flag = tec_synth_new_bodies"
					#	ELEMENT_1_VALUE = 0
					#	ELEMENT_2 = "has_situation_flag = tec_synth_use_robots"
					#	ELEMENT_2_VALUE = -1
					#	ELEMENT_3 = "has_situation_flag = tec_synth_organic_brains"
					#	ELEMENT_3_VALUE = 2
					#	ELEMENT_4 = "has_situation_flag = tec_synth_synthetic_brains"
					#	ELEMENT_4_VALUE = 0
					#	ELEMENT_5 = "has_situation_flag = tec_synth_voluntary_subject"
					#	ELEMENT_5_VALUE = 1
					#	ELEMENT_6 = "has_situation_flag = tec_synth_forced_subject"
					#	ELEMENT_6_VALUE = -1
					#	ELEMENT_7 = "has_situation_flag = tec_synth_slave_subject"
					#	ELEMENT_7_VALUE = -2
					#	ELEMENT_8 = "has_situation_flag = tec_synth_safe_subject"
					#	ELEMENT_8_VALUE = 2
					#}
					set_variable = {
						which = tec_synth_path_score
						value = 0
					}
					# Max 4
					# Neutral -2/2
					# Min -4
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_situation_flag = tec_synth_new_bodies
						}
						change_variable = {
							which = tec_synth_path_score
							value = 0
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_situation_flag = tec_synth_use_robots
						}
						change_variable = {
							which = tec_synth_path_score
							value = -1
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_situation_flag = tec_synth_organic_brains
						}
						change_variable = {
							which = tec_synth_path_score
							value = 2
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_situation_flag = tec_synth_synthetic_brains
						}
						change_variable = {
							which = tec_synth_path_score
							value = 0
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_situation_flag = tec_synth_voluntary_subject
						}
						change_variable = {
							which = tec_synth_path_score
							value = 1
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_situation_flag = tec_synth_forced_subject
						}
						change_variable = {
							which = tec_synth_path_score
							value = -1
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_situation_flag = tec_synth_slave_subject
						}
						change_variable = {
							which = tec_synth_path_score
							value = -2
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_situation_flag = tec_synth_safe_subject
						}
						change_variable = {
							which = tec_synth_path_score
							value = 2
						}
					}
				# /
				# Launch outcomes
					# 2 months so it gives space for the speed to catch up
					if = {	# Bad outcome, -2,-3,-4
						limit = {
							check_variable = {
								which = tec_synth_path_score
								value <= -2
							}
						}
						situation_event = {
							id = tec_synth_path.10073
							days = 60
						}
					}
					else_if = {	# Good, 2,3,4
						limit = {
							check_variable = {
								which = tec_synth_path_score
								value >= 2
							}
						}
						situation_event = {
							id = tec_synth_path.10071
							days = 60
						}
					}
					else = {	# Neutral - 1,0,-1
						situation_event = {
							id = tec_synth_path.10072
							days = 60
						}
					}
				# /
			}
		}

		# Options
			# Regular
			option = {
				name = "tec_synth_path.10070.find.volunteers"
				custom_tooltip = "tec_synth_path.10070.find.volunteers.tooltip"
				icon = {
					icon = GFX_situation_approach_pop
					icon_background = GFX_situation_approach_bg_tec_blue
					text = tec_icon_text_outcome_unknown
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_situation_flag = tec_synth_voluntary_subject
					owner = {
						set_country_flag = tec_synth_voluntary_subject
						random_owned_species = {
							limit = {
								has_citizenship_type = {
									type = citizenship_full
									country = prev
								}
							}
							save_event_target_as = tec_target_species
						}
						random_owned_pop = {
							limit = {
								is_same_species = event_target:tec_target_species
							}
							kill_pop = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			option = {
				name = "tec_synth_path.10070.force.volunteers"
				custom_tooltip = "tec_synth_path.10070.force.volunteers.tooltip"
				icon = {
					icon = GFX_situation_approach_influence
					icon_background = GFX_situation_approach_bg_tec_blue
					text = tec_icon_text_outcome_unknown
				}
				trigger = {
					owner = {
						OR = {
							is_authoritarian = yes
							is_xenophobe = yes
							is_elitist = yes
						}
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_situation_flag = tec_synth_forced_subject
					owner = {
						set_country_flag = tec_synth_forced_subject
						random_owned_species = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									has_citizenship_type = {
										type = citizenship_full
										country = prev
									}
									has_citizenship_type = {
										type = citizenship_limited
										country = prev
									}
								}
							}
							save_event_target_as = tec_target_species
						}
						random_owned_pop = {
							limit = {
								is_same_species = event_target:tec_target_species
							}
							kill_pop = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			option = {

				custom_tooltip = "tec_synth_path.10070.use.enslaved.tooltip"
				icon = {

	situation_event = { # Good 1 - Volunteers offer themselves (pre 50)
		id = tec_synth_path.10011
		title = "tec_synth_path.10011.name"
		desc = "tec_synth_path.10011.desc"

		picture = GFX_evt_scientific_experiments
		show_sound = event_laboratory_sound
		is_triggered_only = yes
		situation = this
		location = target

		trigger = {
			exists = owner
			owner = {
				has_technology = tech_synthetic_workers
				has_technology = tech_synthetic_leaders
			}
		}

		immediate = {
			hidden_effect = {
				set_situation_locked = yes
				owner = {
					# Check organic species
					owner_main_species = {
						save_event_target_as = tec_target_species
					}
					# Check planet
					random_owned_planet = {
						limit = {
							any_owned_species = {
								is_same_species = event_target:tec_target_species
							}
						}
						save_event_target_as = tec_target_planet
					}
				}
			}
		}

		after = {
			hidden_effect = {
				set_situation_locked = no
			}
		}

		option = {
			name = tec_synth_path.10011.a
			custom_tooltip = tec_synth_path.10011.a.tooltip
			icon = {
				icon = GFX_situation_approach_tec_ai
				icon_background = GFX_situation_approach_bg_tec_blue
				text = tec_icon_text_outcome_good
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						situation_progress < 95
					}
					add_situation_progress = 5
				}
				set_timed_situation_flag = {
					flag = tec_situation_bonus_speed
					years = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}

	# TODO ASCENSION MOVE LATER!!!
	country_event = { # Synthetic Evolution
		id = tec_synth_path.105
		title = "tec_synth_path.105.name"
		desc = "tec_synth_path.105.desc"

		picture = GFX_evt_tec_synthetic_first
		show_sound = event_synthetic_evolution
		is_triggered_only = yes

		immediate = {
			set_country_flag = synthetic_empire
		}

		option = {
			name = tec_synth_path.105.a
			custom_tooltip = tec_synth_path.105.a.tooltip
			icon = {
				icon = GFX_situation_approach_tec_ai
				icon_background = GFX_situation_approach_bg_tec_blue
				text = tec_icon_text_outcome_good
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				# Initial finished
				set_country_flag = tec_unlocks_tradition_synthetics
				# Alter species
				tec_create_synth_species_effect = yes
				# TO DO create specific leader ascension trait handler
				every_owned_leader = {
					add_leader_traits_after_modification = yes
					remove_leader_traits_after_modification = yes
				}
				every_pool_leader = {
					add_leader_traits_after_modification = yes
					remove_leader_traits_after_modification = yes
				}
				# Flags
				set_country_flag = tec_synthetic_assimilation
					# Avoid cybogs not being assimilable
				remove_country_flag = tec_cybernetic_t1_assimilation
				remove_country_flag = tec_cybernetic_t2_assimilation
				# Features
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = modifier_tec_free_modification
					days = -1
				}
				fire_on_action = { on_action = tec_ascension_situation_finished }
				# Announcement
				if = {
					limit = {	# Prevents FE and alike from triggering the announce
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = tec_advanced_ascension
						}
					}
					observer_event = { id = observer.4 }
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							is_ai = no
							NOR = {
								is_same_value = root
								# TO DO policy for muting other empire things 
								has_country_flag = tec_mute_empire_announces
							}
							has_communications = root
							root = {
								is_primitive = no
							}
						}
						country_event = { id = utopia.2555 days = 5 }
						country_event = { id = utopia.2556 days = 10 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							any_country = {
								OR = {
									is_country_type = fallen_empire
									is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire
								}
								has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
								has_communications = root
								root = {
									is_primitive = no
								}
								NOT = { is_same_value = root }
							}
						}
						random_country = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									is_country_type = fallen_empire
									is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire
								}
								has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
								has_communications = root
								root = {
									is_primitive = no
								}
								NOT = { is_same_value = root }
							}
							country_event = { id = utopia.2557 days = 15 }
						}
					}
					else = {
						random_country = {
							limit = {
								tec_is_default_country = yes
								has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
								NOT = {
									has_valid_civic = civic_tec_regular_machine_cult
								}
								has_communications = root
								root = {
									is_primitive = no
								}
								NOT = { is_same_value = root }
							}
							country_event = { id = utopia.2557 days = 15 }
						}
						random_country = {
							limit = {
								tec_is_default_country = yes
								is_spiritualist = yes
								has_valid_civic = civic_tec_regular_machine_cult
								has_communications = root
								root = {
									is_primitive = no
								}
								NOT = { is_same_value = root }
							}
							country_event = { id = utopia.25571 days = 15 }
						}
					}
				}
				# Fear of the Dark Separatists - Outraged
					if = {
						limit = {
							any_planet_within_border = {
								has_planet_flag = fotd_seperatist_planet@root
								owner = {
									has_country_flag = fotd_seperatist_country@root
								}
							}
						}
						country_event = { id = origin.6100 days = 10 random = 10 }
					}
				# /
				# Luminary does its thing
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								has_origin = origin_legendary_leader_dictatorial
								AND = {
									has_country_flag = paragon_origin_reformists_gone
									has_origin = origin_legendary_leader_imperial
								}
							}
							NOT = { has_country_flag = luminary_ascension_path }
							exists = ruler
							ruler = { has_leader_flag = paragon_origin_legendary_leader }
						}
						country_event = {
							id = paragon.5201 days = 3600 random = 7200
						}
					}
				# /
			}
		}
	}

	# Tradition - Getting the cybernetic trait or triggering the MAge situation
	country_event = { # T1 Picked Synthetic tradition adoption
		id = tec_synth_path.110
		hide_window = yes

		is_triggered_only = yes

		trigger = {
			has_tradition = tr_synthetics_adopt
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = tec_adopted_tradition_synthetics
			}
		}
		immediate = {
			# Safeproofing flag
			set_country_flag = tec_adopted_tradition_synthetics
			if = {		# MAge - Cyberization situation (regular)
				limit = {
					has_machine_age_dlc = yes
					NOT = {
						has_origin = origin_cybernetic_creed
					}
				}
				if = { # Assimilators
					limit = {
						has_machine_age_dlc = yes
						has_civic = civic_machine_assimilator
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						country_event = {
							id = cyber.2010
							days = 2
						}
					}
				}
				else = { # Non assimilators and etc
					country_event = {
						id = cyber.1
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {	# MAge - Cybernetic creed
				limit = {
					has_machine_age_dlc = yes
					has_origin = origin_cybernetic_creed
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = {
						id = machine_age.100
					}
				}
			}
			else = {	# No MAge - Gives cybernetics
				hidden_effect = {
					# OG is utopia.2500
					country_event = {
						id = tec_cybernetic_path.11010
					}
				}
			}


			# if = {		# MAge - Synthetization situation (regular)
			# 	limit = {
			#
			# 	}
			# }
		}
	}

	# Regular
	country_event = { # T1A Situation completed
		id = tec_psionic_path.105
		title = "tec_psionic_path.105.name"
		desc = "tec_psionic_path.105.desc"
		picture = GFX_evt_psionics
		show_sound = event_mind_over_matter
		trackable = yes

		is_triggered_only = yes

		immediate = {
			hidden_effect = {
				# Initial Finished
				set_country_flag = tec_unlocks_tradition_psionics
				# Alter species
				tec_create_latent_psionic_species_effect = yes
				# TO DO create specific leader ascension trait handler
				every_owned_leader = {
					add_leader_traits_after_modification = yes
					remove_leader_traits_after_modification = yes
				}
				every_pool_leader = {
					add_leader_traits_after_modification = yes
					remove_leader_traits_after_modification = yes
				}
				fire_on_action = { on_action = tec_ascension_situation_finished }
				# Features
				# Fear of the Dark Separatists - Scared
					if = {
						limit = {
							any_planet_within_border = {
								has_planet_flag = fotd_seperatist_planet@root
								owner = {
									has_country_flag = fotd_seperatist_country@root
								}
							}
						}
						country_event = { id = origin.6105 days = 5 random = 2 }
					}
				# /
				# Announcement
				if = {
					limit = {	# Prevents FE and alike from triggering the announce
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = tec_advanced_ascension
						}
					}
					observer_event = { id = observer.5 }
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							is_ai = no
							has_communications = root
							root = {
								is_primitive = no
							}
							NOR = {
								is_same_value = root
								# TO DO policy for muting other empire things 
								has_country_flag = tec_mute_empire_announces
							}
						}
						country_event = {
							id = tec_psionic_path.10501
							days = 5
							random = 2
						}
					}
				}
			}
			# Old code
			if = {
				limit = { always = no }
				every_owned_pop = {
					limit = {
						is_same_species = root
						NOT = { species = { has_trait = trait_latent_psionic } }
					}
					modify_species = {
						species = this
						add_trait = trait_latent_psionic
					}
					species = { save_event_target_as = psionic_species }
				}
				# Ensure the event target exists, since in rare cases the main species is already psionic and no pops get modified
				# (Example: Teachers of the Shroud empires)
				if = {
					limit = {
						exists = event_target:psionic_species
					}
					change_dominant_species = {
						species = event_target:psionic_species
						change_all = yes
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					# Fear of the Dark Separatists - Scared
						if = {
							limit = {
								any_planet_within_border = {
									has_planet_flag = fotd_seperatist_planet@root
									owner = {
										has_country_flag = fotd_seperatist_country@root
									}
								}
							}
							country_event = { id = origin.6105 days = 5 random = 2 }
						}
					# /
					# Announcement
					if = {
						limit = {	# Prevents FE and alike from triggering the announce
							NOT = {
								has_country_flag = tec_advanced_ascension
							}
						}
						observer_event = { id = observer.5 }
						every_country = {
							limit = {
								is_ai = no
								has_communications = root
								root = {
									is_primitive = no
								}
								NOR = {
									is_same_value = root
									# TO DO policy for muting other empire things 
									has_country_flag = tec_mute_empire_announces
								}
							}
							country_event = {
								id = tec_psionic_path.10501
								days = 5
								random = 2
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			# /
		}

		option = {
			name = "tec_psionic_path.105.a"
			custom_tooltip = "tec_psionic_path.105.a.tooltip"
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = tec_unlocks_tradition_psionics
			}
		}

	country_event = { # Psychic Identified - Triggers 5 years after getting latent psi - og utopia.2605
		id = tec_psionic_path.102
		title = "utopia.2605.name"
		desc = "utopia.2605.desc"
		picture = GFX_evt_psionics
		show_sound = event_psionic
		is_triggered_only = yes

		trigger = {
			owner_species = {
				has_trait = trait_latent_psionic
			}
			any_owned_leader = {
				is_same_species = owner_species
				NOR = {
					has_trait = leader_trait_psionic
					has_trait = leader_trait_chosen
					has_chosen_covenant_trait_non_ruler = yes
				}
			}
		}

		immediate = {
			random_owned_leader = {
				limit = {
					is_same_species = owner_species
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = leader_trait_psionic
							has_trait = leader_trait_chosen
							has_chosen_covenant_trait_non_ruler = yes
						}
					}
				}

	country_event = { # T1 picked
		id = tec_machine_path.100
		title = "tec_machine_path.100.name"
		desc = "tec_machine_path.100.desc"
		picture = GFX_evt_machine_sapience
		show_sound = event_synthetic_evolution
		trackable = yes

		is_triggered_only = yes

		option = {
			name = "tec_machine_path.100.a"
			custom_tooltip = "tec_machine_path.100.a.tooltip"
			hidden_effect = {
				save_event_target_as = tec_target_country
				event_target:tec_target_country = {
					start_situation = {
						type = situation_tec_machine_path_t1
						target = event_target:tec_target_country.capital_scope
						effect = {
							save_event_target_as = new_situation
						}
					}
					event_target:new_situation = {
						set_situation_locked = no
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
  # /
  # ---------------  MACHINE T1 Situation
